[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+       [0m[39mu.i = [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint64_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mhx<<[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m | [0m[1;39m([0m[39mu.i&[0m[1;36m0xffffffff[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+       [0m[39mx = u.f;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+       [0m[39mf = x - [0m[1;36m1.0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+       [0m[39mhfsq = [0m[1;36m0.5[0m[39m*f*f;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+       [0m[39ms = f/[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2.0[0m[39m+f[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+       [0m[35m/[0m[39m* See log2.c for details. *[0m[35m/[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+       [0m[35m/[0m[39m* hi+lo = f - hfsq + s*[0m[1;39m([0m[39mhfsq+R[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ~ [0m[1;35mlog[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m+f[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+       [0m[39mu.i &= [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint64_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m<<[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+       [0m[39mhi = u.f;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIf the diff is not related to the current issue, you can ignore it.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mrelated_diff[0m[39m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA one‐byte stack buffer overflow was detected in the custom floating‐point [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformatting branch of `mg_vxprintf` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min `src/fmt.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, triggered when the fuzzer [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexercised the `%e` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexponential[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m format specifier. AddressSanitizer reports a write[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeyond the end of a local [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m‐byte buffer used for temporary formatting data.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During fuzz testing, AddressSanitizer flags a stack-buffer-overflow in the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction `mg_pfn_iobuf_private`, which is called indirectly by `mg_vxprintf` when [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing the `%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E` conversion. The overflow occurs at an offset of [0m[1;36m120[0m[39m bytes [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the `mg_vxprintf` stack frame, specifically overrunning a temporary array [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`tmp371`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m defined in that function.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This is a classic stack-based buffer overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCWE-[0m[1;36m121[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. A one‐byte write is [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperformed past the end of a local character buffer used for building the exponent [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpart of a floating‐point number.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The crash trace shows the write originates in the new `%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E` formatting [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbranch inside `mg_vxprintf` [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`src/fmt.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, not in unrelated parser or harness code.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Two local arrays exist in that frame [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`tmp` and `tmp371`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, each of limited [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize; the write overruns `tmp371` by one byte.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The added code uses `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` to hold formatted mantissa and exponent [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpieces without checking that the assembled string, including the sign, decimal [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpoint, exponent digits, and terminator, actually fits.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. The overflow is surfaced by logging inside `mg_http_parse` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min `src/http.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich invokes `mg_log`, then `mg_vxprintf`.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Investigation Scope  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To fully understand the impact and root context, the following areas should be [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexamined:  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The new `%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E` case in `mg_vxprintf` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min both `src/fmt.c` and `src/fmt.h`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparticularly buffer sizing and write logic.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Supporting routines `mg_dtoa` and `mg_lld` used to convert mantissa and [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexponent.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The implementation of `scpy` and `mg_pfn_iobuf_private` which perform the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mactual buffered writes.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Call sites such as `mg_log` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min `src/log.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `mg_http_parse` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/http.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m where formatted output is generated.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Any assumptions about maximum field width or precision that could limit the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize of the formatted exponent.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The AddressSanitizer trace shows a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m‐byte stack overflow in the `%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbranch of `mg_vxprintf` when writing to the local array `tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In that branch, two formatting routines are called in sequence:  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m `[0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` produces the mantissa digits plus[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma terminating `[0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m`. With [0m[33mprecision[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m this can emit up to [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m digit, a decimal [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpoint, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m fractional digits, and the `[0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m`—potentially [0m[1;36m11[0m[39m bytes.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m `[0m[1;35mmg_lld[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, exponent, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` also writes a null‐terminated string for the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexponent.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Both calls assume that the caller’s buffer is large enough to hold the string [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mplus its terminator. However, `tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` is too small, so `mg_dtoa` overruns by at [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleast one byte [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe `[0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and triggers the sanitizer failure.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Critical Logic to Preserve  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The parsing logic of the `%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E` specifier in `mg_vxprintf`, including: [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextracting the `double`, computing its base‐[0m[1;36m10[0m[39m exponent [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia `[0m[1;35mlog10[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mmy_fabs[0m[1;39m([0m[39md[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mscaling to a normalized mantissa, calling `mg_dtoa` with [0m[33mprecision[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, emitting the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformat specifier character itself, and calling `mg_lld` for the exponent.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The behavior and signature of the public `mg_*printf` APIs must remain [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged, including how they route to `mg_vxprintf` and how they use `scpy` to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutput.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Proposed Patch Outline  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m In `src/fmt.c`, locate the `%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E` branch in `mg_vxprintf` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m314[0m[39m and again around [0m[1;36m718[0m[39m in the posted diff[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Replace `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;` with a larger local buffer, e.g.:  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m before:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m    char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m after:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m16[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      or, for extra safety, `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m32[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;`  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m No other changes to the logic—both `mg_dtoa` and `mg_lld` will now have [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msufficient space for their full output plus terminator.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Recompile and rerun the existing unit tests and fuzz harness; the overflow [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould disappear without altering any external behavior.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Allocating at least [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand preferably [0m[1;36m32[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m guarantees that:  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - `mg_dtoa` can emit up to ~[0m[1;36m11[0m[39m characters [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;39m[[0m[39m-[0m[1;39m][0m[39md.dddddddd\[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m safely.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - `mg_lld` can emit up to ~[0m[1;36m5[0m[39m characters [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;39m[[0m[39m-[0m[1;39m][0m[39mddd\[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m safely.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to external APIs, test code, or fuzz harness.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The change is localized, preserving all existing formatting logic and flags.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Additional stack usage [0m[1;39m([0m[39m~[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m24[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is negligible.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Slight increase in stack usage in `mg_vxprintf`, which is called for every [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformatted output. However, a [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m‐byte bump on the stack is minimal and should not[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimpact typical embedded or server workloads.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No change to runtime paths or to how `mg_dtoa`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`mg_lld` behave beyond removing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe overflow.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Verification Steps  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rebuild and run the full unit test suite; no failures should occur.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Re‐run the AddressSanitizer‐enabled fuzz targets for `%e` formatting; the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mone‐byte overflow should be eliminated.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Optionally, add a targeted unit test for an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m‐digit fractional `%e` case [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39me.g., `[0m[1;35mmg_snprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, size, [0m[32m"%e"[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m1.23456789[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to ensure correct output and no[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIf the diff is not related to the current issue, you can ignore it.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mrelated_diff[0m[39m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe initial issue is an AddressSanitizer-detected stack-buffer-overflow in the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_vxprintf` path when handling scientific notation [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  A custom [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformatting branch was added, introducing small local buffers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhold mantissa and exponent strings.  The overflow occurs when those buffers are too[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msmall for certain inputs.  A patch attempt enlarged the first buffer to [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m bytes [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m32[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and updated the call to `mg_dtoa` accordingly.  After rebuilding [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand rerunning the fuzzer, the same one-byte stack-buffer-overflow still occurs in a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecond unnamed temporary buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`tmp371`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating that not all local buffers [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwere adjusted.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A libFuzzer run on Mongoose’s HTTP parser triggered an AddressSanitizer error in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_pfn_iobuf_private`, called via `mg_vxprintf`.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The crash stack trace shows a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write just past a stack buffer in the frame [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor `mg_vxprintf` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min `fmt.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- AddressSanitizer reports two local objects in that frame:  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `tmp` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbytes at offsets [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m72[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `tmp371` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbytes at offsets [0m[1;36m112[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m120[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow is at offset [0m[1;36m120[0m[39m, just past the end of `tmp371`.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The code path for `%e` formatting [0m[1;39m([0m[39madded by a diff[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m allocates `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, uses[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to write to it, then calls `[0m[1;35mmg_lld[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexponent, …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` also writing to it.  Neither buffer size nor the calls guarantee that[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe output will fit in [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes, leading to the overflow.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In `src/fmt.c`, the local buffer for `%e` handling was changed from `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m32[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The call to `mg_dtoa` was updated to `[0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmatching the new buffer size.  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes were made to the second temporary buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`tmp371`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that is also [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m190[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!tz && n > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m targ_width = width + n;[0m                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m196[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m197[0m[39m:  [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/fmt.[0m[1;92mc:317[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m328[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m317[0m[39m:      [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc == [0m[32m'e'[0m[39m || c == [0m[32m'E'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m318[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m  char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m319[0m[39m:          double d = [0m[1;35mva_arg[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*ap, double[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m320[0m[39m:          int64_t exponent = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint64_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mlog10[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mmy_fabs[0m[1;39m([0m[39md[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m321[0m[39m:          double mantissa = d [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;35mpower[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, exponent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m322[0m[39m:          k = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m323[0m[39m:          n += [0m[1;35mscpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout, param, tmp, k[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m324[0m[39m:          [0m[1;35mout[0m[1;39m([0m[39mc, param[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m325[0m[39m:          n++;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m326[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m  k = [0m[1;35mmg_lld[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, exponent, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m327[0m[39m:          n += [0m[1;35mscpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout, param, tmp, k[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m328[0m[39m:    [0m[39m  [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc == [0m[32m'%'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Analyze Root Cause[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The stack-buffer-overflow arises in the `%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E` formatting branch of [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_vxprintf` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min `src/fmt.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which uses a fixed-size local buffer `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtwice:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • First, to hold the mantissa string produced by `[0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m, …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Second, to hold the exponent string produced by `[0m[1;35mmg_lld[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, exponent, …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The overflow occurs because:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • A mantissa with [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m digit, a decimal point and up to [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m fractional digits can [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe up to [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m characters [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `[0m[32m"9.99999999"[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, plus the terminating `[0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m` written [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby `mg_snprintf` inside `mg_dtoa`, requiring at least [0m[1;36m11[0m[39m bytes.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • The exponent may be up to [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m digits plus a sign [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `[0m[32m"-308"[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, requiring [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mup to [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - AddressSanitizer reports two local arrays in the `mg_vxprintf` frame:  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • The first `tmp` [0m[1;39m([0m[39moffsets [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m72[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, enlarged in the prior patch from [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m to [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes but still not large enough for the mantissa + null in worst cases.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • The second buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`tmp371`, offsets [0m[1;36m112[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m120[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes and overflows [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mon the exponent formatting.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Critical Logic to Preserve[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The existing call sequence:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       k = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, dstlen, mantissa, precision, [0m[33mc[0m[39m==[0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mscpy[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, tmp, k[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mout[0m[1;39m([0m[39mc, param[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       k = [0m[1;35mmg_lld[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, exponent, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mscpy[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, tmp, k[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The use of `[0m[1;35mscpy[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich iterates up to `len` or until `[0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m must remain [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged to preserve the way characters are emitted.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Avoid changes to harness or fuzzing logic; only modify `src/fmt.c` inside [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_vxprintf`.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Retain formatting semantics exactly [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmantissa first, then the `e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`E` [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcharacter, then the exponent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Strategy to Fix the Overflow[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Unify and Enlarge the Temporary Buffer[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Replace all instances of `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` in the `%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E` [0m[1;35mbranch[0m[1;39m([0m[39mes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m of [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_vxprintf` with a single, sufficiently large array, for example:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m16[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        – [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m bytes safely covers:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           • Up to [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m chars for mantissa [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[32m"d.dddddddd"[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, plus a `[0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m` = [0m[1;36m11[0m[39m [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes,[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           • Up to [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m chars for exponent [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. `[0m[32m"-999"[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           • One extra margin.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - If desired, use `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m32[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` for extra safety, but [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m bytes is sufficient[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgiven worst-case conversion lengths.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Parameterize Buffer Length in `mg_dtoa`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Replace hardcoded `[0m[33mdstlen[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m10[0m[39m` in the `mg_dtoa` call with the actual buffer [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          k = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, mantissa, precision, [0m[33mc[0m[39m==[0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This change ensures `mg_dtoa` never writes more characters than the buffer [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcan hold.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Adjust the Exponent Formatting Invocation[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - The call to `[0m[1;35mmg_lld[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, exponent, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` writes at most [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m characters [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnull[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Since we use `[0m[1;35mscpy[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, tmp, k[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `k` excludes the null, no additional [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnull write occurs. The enlarged `tmp` still accommodates this safely.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Locate and Patch All `%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E` Branches[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In some builds, `mg_vxprintf` may be specialized or duplicated by macro. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIdentify every `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[33m...[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` in every `%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E` branch [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., in generic code and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39many `.specialized` clones[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and apply the same buffer enlargement and `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madjustment. This addresses both the original `tmp` and the second buffer [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`tmp371`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Step-by-Step Implementation[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `src/fmt.c` and locate the `mg_vxprintf` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m300[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Find the clause:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc == [0m[32m'e'[0m[39m || c == [0m[32m'E'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            …[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            k = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, [0m[33mc[0m[39m==[0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            …[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            k = [0m[1;35mmg_lld[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, exponent, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            …[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Change `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;` → `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m16[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m if preferred[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Change the `mg_dtoa` call to:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        k = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, [0m[33mc[0m[39m==[0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Ensure the `mg_lld` call remains as-is [0m[1;39m([0m[39mit returns a length, `scpy` uses it[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Search for any other `%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E` branches or duplicated code [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., in [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_vxprintf.specialized`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and apply the same edits.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m. Rebuild and rerun the fuzzer to confirm the ASan error is resolved.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification & Side-Effect Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By sizing `tmp` to at least [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m bytes and passing `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to `mg_dtoa`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwe eliminate the possibility that `mg_dtoa` overruns the buffer.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `mg_lld` call writes only up to [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m characters, well within [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m bytes.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No new code paths or logic changes are introduced; existing formatting [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior and the `scpy`-based emission remain untouched.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This patch does not alter any external or harness code and preserves all [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39munit and fuzz[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If future format precision grows, the use of `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` guards against [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhardcoded mismatches.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Verification[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After patching, rebuild the library and re-run the libFuzzer suite for at [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleast [0m[1;36m1000[0m[39m iterations.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm no AddressSanitizer reports for `mg_vxprintf`.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run unit tests, including any added checks for `%e` formatting [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`test_mg_snprintf`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, to ensure output correctness and buffer safety.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSummary[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Enlarge all local `tmp` buffers in the `%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E` branch of `mg_vxprintf` to at[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleast [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m bytes.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace hardcoded `dstlen` in `mg_dtoa` with `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure all duplicated/specialized formatting branches receive the same fix.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis single patch addresses both the original mantissa overflow and the secondary [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexponent-buffer overflow in one coherent change.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
